Talent Acquisition Executive

Company Overview

KOTT Software Pvt. Ltd. is a well-established, ISO 9001:2015-certified, 100% EOU company specializing in offshore software development and enterprise product development since 1997. We deliver client-centric, robust business solutions and are recognized as industry leaders.

Role Summary

We seek a skilled HR professional to oversee our end-to-end recruitment cycle. The ideal candidate will have IT/technology awareness, collaborate with stakeholders, develop recruitment strategies, and build strong talent pipelines for current and future hiring needs.

Responsibilities - Source candidates via online portals, job boards, social media, and print media. - Coordinate with hiring managers to define resource requirements and selection criteria. - Manage hiring processes using Applicant Tracking Systems (ATS). - Screen candidates via calls/emails, conduct pre-interview assessments, and facilitate interviews. - Monitor HR metrics (time-to-fill, time-to-hire, source of hire). - Assist with HR administration, employee onboarding, and statutory filings. - Organize travel, training, and team-building events. - Maintain HR documents and promote a collaborative, accountable workplace culture.

Requirements - Minimum 2 years of experience as an IT recruiter. - Proven expertise in full-cycle recruitment (360-degree/end-to-end). - Technical understanding of IT roles and pre-screening skills. - Knowledge of sourcing techniques (e.g., Boolean search, social media recruiting). - Familiarity with job boards (Naukri, Indeed, LinkedIn) and ATS tools. - Excellent communication, organizational, and multitasking abilities. - MBA in HR Management, IT, or a related field preferred. - Creative problem-solving mindset and proactive attitude.

Contact

Interested candidates should email their updated resume to careers@kottsoftware.com.

Role Overview

We seek a Senior AI Engineer (Generative AI & Deployment) to design, develop, and deploy production-grade Generative AI systems. This role requires deep technical expertise and independent ownership of the AI model lifecycle, from research to scalable deployment, collaborating with the Lead AI Engineer and cross-functional teams.

Ideal Background

  • Master’s degree (or equivalent) in Computer Science, AI, ML, or related fields.
  • 5–8 years of AI/ML engineering experience with end-to-end model development/deployment.
  • Python proficiency (mandatory).
  • Vector Databases (pgvector, Pinecone, Weaviate, Milvus) experience (mandatory).
  • Relational Databases (PostgreSQL, MySQL, SQL Server) knowledge (mandatory).
  • Frameworks: PyTorch, TensorFlow, Hugging Face Transformers.
  • LLM fine-tuning, transformer architectures, and generative AI models.
  • MLOps expertise (CI/CD, model monitoring, deployment pipelines).
  • Cloud deployment (AWS/GCP/Azure).
  • Ability to work independently and communicate technical concepts clearly.

Key Responsibilities

  • Design and optimize LLMs, RAG pipelines, and transformer-based solutions.
  • Apply advanced knowledge of Vector DBs, Python, and RDBMS for scalable AI systems.
  • Fine-tune models, run experiments, and iterate to production quality.
  • Implement MLOps best practices for reliable, monitored AI systems.
  • Build RAG and agentic AI pipelines for enterprise SaaS products.
  • Optimize model efficiency, reduce latency, and scale systems.
  • Collaborate with product managers, engineers, and data scientists.
  • Stay current with AI/ML research and prototype solutions.
  • Write clean, documented code and participate in code reviews.

Preferred Skills

  • WebSocket-based AI communication and real-time inference.
  • Experience with Chatbots, CRM, ERP, Accounting, and HRTech systems.
  • Knowledge of Responsible AI, governance, and compliance.
  • LangChain, LlamaIndex, or similar orchestration frameworks.
  • Prompt engineering, few-shot learning, instruction tuning.
  • Multi-modal AI models (vision, audio, document understanding).
  • Material UI, multi-theme applications, and UX for AI products.

Benefits & Perks

  • Competitive compensation with performance incentives.
  • Global career pathways across UAE, KSA, UK, Qatar, India.
  • Health & wellness benefits (insurance, well-being programs).
  • On-site role at Infopark, Kochi.

Apply by: 30 Apr 2026

Data Engineer/Database Administrator (DBA)

We are seeking a skilled Database Administrator (DBA) professional with strong expertise in database management, data security, and governance, along with experience in enterprise data integration.

The ideal candidate will be responsible for ensuring the performance, availability, security, and compliance of database systems, while also supporting data engineering initiatives such as data integration and pipeline development. This role plays a critical part in safeguarding enterprise data, enforcing governance standards, and enabling reliable analytics across the organization.

Key Responsibilities:

  • Manage, monitor, and maintain database systems across cloud and hybrid environments, ensuring high availability, performance, and reliability.
  • Perform database performance tuning, query optimization, indexing, and capacity planning.
  • Design and implement backup, recovery, and disaster recovery strategies.
  • Implement and enforce data security practices, including role-based access control (RBAC), encryption (at rest and in transit), and access management.
  • Apply data masking and anonymization techniques to protect sensitive and confidential data.
  • Enforce data governance policies, standards, and compliance requirements (e.g., GDPR) across database systems.
  • Monitor, audit, and track database access, usage, and security events to ensure compliance and risk mitigation.
  • Plan and execute database migrations, upgrades, and patching activities.
  • Support ETL/ELT processes and data integration workflows across enterprise systems.
  • Handle and support ingestion of structured, semi-structured, and unstructured data, including databases, files (CSV, JSON, XML), and document-based formats (PDFs, images, audio).
  • Collaborate with data engineers and architects to design scalable and optimized data architectures and storage solutions.
  • Ensure alignment between database design, data pipelines, and business requirements.
  • Maintain documentation for database configurations, security controls, and operational procedures.

Required Qualifications:

  • 5+ years of experience as a Database Administrator (DBA) with exposure to data engineering principles.
  • Strong expertise in:
  • Database performance tuning, query optimization, and indexing
  • Backup, recovery, and disaster recovery strategies
  • High availability and reliability of database systems
  • Hands-on experience with data security practices, including:
  • Role-based access control (RBAC)
  • Encryption (at rest and in transit)
  • User and access management
  • Experience implementing data masking or anonymization techniques for sensitive data.
  • Solid understanding of data governance principles and compliance requirements (e.g., GDPR, ISO 27001).
  • Advanced proficiency in SQL and working knowledge of Python (or similar scripting language).
  • Experience working with relational database systems (e.g., SQL Server, Oracle, PostgreSQL, MySQL).
  • Familiarity with ETL/ELT processes and data integration concepts.
  • Experience handling structured, semi-structured, and unstructured data (e.g., JSON, XML, PDFs, images).

Preferred Qualifications:

  • Experience with cloud-based database platforms (preferably Microsoft Azure or equivalent).
  • Relevant certifications such as Microsoft Certified: Azure Database Administrator Associate or relevant.
  • Familiarity with data protection regulations and compliance frameworks (e.g., GDPR, ISO 27001) and their implementation.
  • Experience with database monitoring, auditing, and security tools.
  • Exposure to supporting data engineering or analytics teams in enterprise environments.

Infopark

5+ YearsICD-10-CMCPTSurgical Coding
Apply by: 05 May 2026

Senior Coding Officer

Job Summary

The Inpatient (IP) DRG Medical Coder is responsible for accurately assigning diagnostic and procedural codes to inpatient medical records based on the guidelines provided by the International Classification of Diseases (ICD), Current Procedural Terminology (CPT), and Diagnosis-Related Group (DRG) coding systems. The coder ensures that the codes assigned are accurate, compliance with DOH regulations and insurance requirements.

Key Responsibilities

  • Review and analyze patient records: Examine doctors' notes, medical documents, diagnostic reports, drug administration charts, and other records ensuring that all diagnoses and procedures are properly documented.
  • Assign codes: Use ICD 10 CM (International Classification of Diseases - 2021 guidelines) and CPT (Current Procedural Terminology - 2021 guidelines) and E&M (Evaluation and Management - 2018 guidelines) systems to assign standardized codes.
  • DRG Assignment: Determine the appropriate DRG for each inpatient case based on the primary and secondary diagnoses, procedures, and other clinical data in the medical record.
  • Compliance: Ensure coding practices are in full compliance with DOH regulations and Daman, ADNIC, and other payer-specific guidelines. Follow all coding conventions and guidelines outlined by ICD-10, CPT, and DRG protocols.
  • Medical Record Review: Review physician and clinical documentation to ensure completeness, accuracy, and clarity, and query healthcare providers when necessary to clarify or complete documentation.
  • Coding Audits: Perform coding audits and reviews to identify discrepancies, errors, or opportunities for improvement in coding accuracy.
  • Billing and Reimbursement Support: Collaborate with the billing department to ensure correct coding for billing purposes and support accurate claims submissions for reimbursement.
  • Ensure accuracy: Verify that all codes are accurate and compliant with regulations.
  • Responsible for submitting claims with appropriate primary diagnosis, secondary diagnosis, primary procedures, secondary procedure codes, appropriate modifiers, and DRG.
  • Responsible for maintaining accuracy of 97% in internal audits.
  • Maintain confidentiality: Uphold strict confidentiality in line with DOH guidelines and ensure patient information is kept confidential.

Qualifications

  • Education: Associate's or Bachelor's degree in Health Information Management, Health Information Technology, or a related field.
  • Certifications: Preferred certifications include Certified Coding Specialist (CCS), Certified Inpatient Coder (CIC), or Certified Professional Coder (CPC) certification or any other coding certifications from AAPC or AHIMA.
  • Skills:
  • Strong knowledge of ICD-10-CM, CPT, and DRG coding systems.
  • Ability to read and understand medical records and clinical terminology.
  • Familiarity with coding and billing software, electronic health records (EHR) systems, and coding tools.
  • Good Knowledge in Surgical coding (UAE or US)
  • Strong analytical and problem-solving skills.
  • Excellent communication skills for collaboration with clinical staff and for clarification purposes.

Role Purpose

Deliver dependable Python automation and advanced analytics that support our reporting products, reducing manual effort, increasing data quality, and improving insight timeliness. Emphasize maintainable code, defensible logic, controlled execution, monitoring, and repeatable outputs.

Responsibilities

Essential Functions

  • Python Automation Development:
  • Design, develop, test, and maintain Python scripts that automate repeatable analytics and reporting workflows supporting Power BI dashboards and operational reporting deliverables.

  • Integrations (APIs / Workflow Tools / Reporting Enablement):

  • Integrate Python automation with approved workflow tools for controlled publishing and operational handoffs.

  • Ensure integration code follows security and governance expectations (controlled access, credential handling, auditability).

  • Documentation, Standards, and Maintainability:

  • Document automation and analytics design, inputs/outputs, dependencies, run instructions, and troubleshooting steps.
  • Maintain code repositories with version control practices and clear change notes.
  • Create runbooks for operational handoffs and ensure another developer can support the automation if needed.
  • Support dashboard development by delivering clean, well-defined analytical outputs and validation signals the BI layer can consume and explain.
  • Participate in stakeholder discussions as needed to clarify analytical requirements and acceptance criteria.

About Us

Way.com is building the ecosystem and marketplace for everyday mobility. Way saves drivers money and earns them rewards on everyday things for their cars – car washes, parking, gas, and insurance – while providing roadside assistance and towing when things go wrong. With millions of transactions and a growing network of partner locations across the US, Way is redefining how drivers care for their vehicles. Featured by Bloomberg and ranked 48th on Andreessen Horowitz’s Marketplace list of fastest-growing companies worldwide and recognized as the top Product in Insurance by UnitQ, we’re making car ownership easier, more affordable, and more rewarding.

Role Overview

We are seeking a Creative Director who can think, create, and lead – someone who brings agency-caliber creative thinking to an in-house role with real business ownership. This role owns the end-to-end development of marketing and advertising campaigns from concept to execution, across multiple channels and product lines. You will partner with the Omnichannel Marketing Lead on campaign strategy and priorities, but you own the creative vision – from the initial concept and tagline through to the final delivered assets.

Key Responsibilities

  • Lead end-to-end campaign creation across digital, social, video, print, OOH, and email

  • Develop creative for co-branded campaigns with Way’s partner network (e.g. car wash operators, parking facilities)

Creative Direction & Concept

  • Develop campaign ideas, narratives, taglines, and messaging that capture the spirit of the brand and drive consumer action
  • Simplify complex, multi-product services into clear, engaging communication that resonates with US consumers

Performance-Oriented Creative

  • Partner closely with the omnichannel marketing team to align creative output with campaign goals and conversion targets
  • Iterate based on data, A/B testing, and performance insights – creative decisions should be informed by results, not just instinct

Team Leadership

  • Lead, mentor, and grow a team of designers, copywriters, and motion/video specialists
  • Manage freelancers and external creative partners, ensuring quality and brand alignment across all contributors

Hands-on Execution

  • Contribute directly to design, copy, or creative direction when required – this is not a review-only role
  • Ensure final output matches creative intent and meets quality standards across every deliverable

Stakeholder Collaboration

  • Present creative concepts and campaign strategies to US-based leadership and internal stakeholders
  • Clearly articulate the rationale behind creative decisions and incorporate feedback without losing the creative vision

Preferred Skills

  • 8+ years in a Creative Director or Senior Art Director role at a full-service advertising agency
  • Strong portfolio showcasing complete, multi-channel campaign work from concept through delivery
  • Proven ability to execute omnichannel campaigns across digital, social, video, print, OOH, and email
  • Strong conceptual thinking and copywriting ability – can craft taglines, headlines, and campaign narratives that drive action
  • Experience marketing US-facing consumer brands while based in India, with a strong understanding of American consumer behavior and cultural nuances
  • Proficiency in Adobe Creative Suite, Figma, and video/motion tools – capable of producing, not just directing
  • Experience managing and mentoring creative teams, including working with freelancers and vendors across time zones
  • Understanding of performance marketing and conversion-focused design – knows how to create work that moves metrics, not just wins awards
  • Ability to thrive in a fast-paced, high-volume environment managing multiple simultaneous campaigns across different product lines
  • Strong presentation and communication skills – can pitch creative concepts to US-based stakeholders and articulate the “why” behind every decision

What We Look For

  • Clear thinking over complexity – you simplify, you don’t complicate
  • Ownership over delegation – you see it through, not just hand it off
  • Speed with quality – you move fast without cutting corners
  • Creative that delivers business outcomes, not just aesthetics – beautiful work that also converts

What This Role Is (and Isn’t)

This is a hands-on creative leadership role with full accountability for both the quality of the work and its business impact. You will concept, create, and ship – not just review and approve. If you’re looking for a role where you direct from the sidelines, this isn’t it. If you want to build a creative function from the ground up and see your work drive real results at scale in the US market, this is the role.

Why Join Way.com

  • Work on products used at scale in the US market – your creative will reach millions of drivers
  • Lead campaigns across multiple verticals (car wash, parking, gas, insurance) in one unified ecosystem
  • Full creative autonomy to shape campaigns from concept to completion
  • Opportunity to build and grow your own creative team
  • Be part of a team where design directly impacts business growth – not a cost center, a growth driver
